# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
So, the general algorithm is: ^m6Krqs8g

Count the possible positions for the repeated pair (adjacent 2s): 3 ^WqxUvXA5

Count the arrangements of the remaining digits: 2 ^mgFbYJUT

Multiply: 3 × 2 = 6 ^4nJ8Kxan

Find the number of distinguishable arrangements of the letters of the word. ^3u3mXOBe

QUINTILLION ^Y4cPDUW2
